   Registry SDs are stored by registryd alongside key data
P  registry_access_via_impersonation  §9.11 L3924–3926
   registryd enforces access control by impersonating the client and calling AccessCheck via KACS syscall
P  kernel_objects_sd_inline  §9.11 L3933–3934
   Kernel object SDs (tokens, processes, logon sessions) are stored inline on the kernel object
P  kernel_object_sd_set_at_creation  §9.11 L3935–3936
   Kernel object SDs are typically set at object creation time
P  ipc_endpoints_sd_owned_by_service  §9.11 L3938–3939
   IPC endpoint SDs are stored by the service that owns the endpoint

   When a client connects to an IPC endpoint, the service calls AccessCheck with client token and endpoint SD before accepting
---

## Summary
**Classification rationale:** The vast majority of §9 tests are Cargo tests because Security Descriptors are pure data structures — parsing, serialization, format validation, inheritance computation, ACE ordering, conditional expression evaluation, and access mask manipulation are all pure Rust logic testable without a kernel. The Provium tests are concentrated in §9.5 re-propagation (requires a live filesystem tree walk), §9.7 ownership transfer (requires actual privilege checks through syscalls), and §9.11 storage (requires xattr I/O, LSM blob caching, registryd impersonation, and IPC endpoint behavior in a running system).

---

# Section 11: AccessCheck (First Half)
## AccessCheck Test Corpus -- Section 11 (First Half)
### 11.1 API Variants
C  access_check_tree_requires_all_nodes_pass  11.1
   AccessCheck with object type list fails if any node is denied
C  access_check_tree_granted_is_intersection  11.1, 11.17
   AccessCheck with tree returns root.granted (intersection of all nodes)
C  access_check_result_list_requires_tree  11.1, 11.17
   AccessCheckResultList without object_tree returns ERROR_INVALID_PARAMETER
C  access_check_result_list_per_node_verdict  11.1
   AccessCheckResultList returns per-node granted/status independently
C  access_check_result_list_partial_denial  11.1
   AccessCheckResultList: denial on one property fails only that property, not the whole request
C  access_check_result_list_max_allowed_returns_per_node_granted  11.17
   AccessCheckResultList in MAXIMUM_ALLOWED mode returns node.granted per node
C  access_check_result_list_normal_mode_returns_desired_or_zero  11.17
   AccessCheckResultList in normal mode returns mapped_desired for OK nodes, 0 for denied nodes
### 11.2 Generic Mapping
C  generic_read_maps_to_specific_bits  11.2
   GENERIC_READ in desired mask maps to mapping.read and clears bit 31
C  generic_write_maps_to_specific_bits  11.2
   GENERIC_WRITE in desired mask maps to mapping.write and clears bit 30
C  generic_execute_maps_to_specific_bits  11.2
   GENERIC_EXECUTE in desired mask maps to mapping.execute and clears bit 29
C  generic_all_maps_to_specific_bits  11.2
   GENERIC_ALL in desired mask maps to mapping.all and clears bit 28
C  multiple_generic_bits_map_simultaneously  11.2
   Multiple generic bits in desired map all at once (OR of all mapped sets)
C  generic_bits_never_in_comparisons  11.2
   After mapping, no generic bits remain in the desired mask
C  mapped_desired_used_for_success_verdict  11.2
   The success/failure verdict compares granted against mapped_desired, not original desired
C  ace_mask_mapped_defensively_during_walk  11.2, 11.3
   ACE masks in the DACL are mapped through MapGenericBits at evaluation time (not at SD creation)
C  ace_mask_mapping_uses_local_copy  11.2, 11.3
   ACE mask mapping does not mutate the original ACE (uses local copy)
C  map_generic_bits_noop_if_no_generic_bits  11.2
   MapGenericBits is a no-op when input has no generic bits set
C  generic_bits_in_ace_mask_work_after_mapping  11.2, 11.3
   An ACE with GENERIC_READ in its mask grants the mapped-specific bits, not bit 31
### 11.3 DACL Walk -- Core Mechanics
C  allow_ace_grants_undecided_bits  11.3
   Allow ACE grants rights for bits not yet decided
C  deny_ace_denies_undecided_bits  11.3
   Deny ACE marks bits as decided-but-not-granted for undecided bits
C  first_writer_wins_deny_before_allow  11.3
   A deny ACE preceding an allow ACE for the same bits: deny wins
C  first_writer_wins_allow_before_deny  11.3
   An allow ACE preceding a deny ACE for the same bits: allow wins
C  already_decided_bits_unaffected_by_later_allow  11.3
   An allow ACE cannot override bits already decided (either granted or denied)
C  already_decided_bits_unaffected_by_later_deny  11.3
   A deny ACE cannot override bits already decided (either granted or denied)
C  each_bit_decided_at_most_once  11.3
   Each bit position is resolved at most once during the DACL walk
C  non_canonical_order_respects_position  11.3
   Non-canonical ACE ordering (allow before deny) grants via first-writer-wins
C  no_hard_failure_on_denial  11.3
   Denials during the walk are recorded as decided-not-granted, not errors
### 11.3 DACL Walk -- SID Matching
C  allow_ace_matches_user_sid  11.3
   Allow ACE with token's user SID matches
C  allow_ace_matches_enabled_group  11.3
   Allow ACE matches a group SID that has SE_GROUP_ENABLED
C  allow_ace_skips_deny_only_group  11.3
   Allow ACE does NOT match a group with USE_FOR_DENY_ONLY
C  deny_ace_matches_deny_only_group  11.3
   Deny ACE DOES match a group with USE_FOR_DENY_ONLY
C  deny_ace_matches_enabled_group  11.3
   Deny ACE matches a group with SE_GROUP_ENABLED
C  neither_enabled_nor_deny_only_skipped  11.3
   A group with neither ENABLED nor USE_FOR_DENY_ONLY is invisible to both allow and deny ACEs
C  user_sid_deny_only_blocks_allow  11.3
   Token with user SID marked deny-only: user SID matches deny ACEs but not allow ACEs
C  user_sid_deny_only_matches_deny  11.3
   Token with user SID marked deny-only: deny ACE targeting user SID fires
C  ace_sid_no_match_skipped  11.3
   ACE whose SID matches neither user SID nor any group SID is skipped
C  deny_only_group_blocks_access_via_deny_ace  11.3, 11.7
   A deny-only group triggers deny ACEs that block access but cannot grant via allow ACEs
### 11.3 DACL Walk -- Special Cases
C  inherit_only_ace_skipped  11.3
   ACE with INHERIT_ONLY flag is skipped during the DACL walk
C  null_dacl_grants_all_valid_bits  11.3
   SD with SE_DACL_PRESENT clear grants all valid rights (via MapGenericBits(GENERIC_ALL))
C  null_dacl_does_not_grant_garbage_bits  11.3
   NULL DACL grants MapGenericBits(GENERIC_ALL, mapping), not raw 0xFFFFFFFF
C  null_dacl_respects_already_decided  11.3
   NULL DACL only grants bits not already decided by earlier pipeline stages
C  empty_dacl_grants_nothing  11.3
   DACL present with zero ACEs: no rights are granted by the walk
C  short_circuit_when_all_desired_decided  11.3
   Walk stops early when all bits in desired are decided (optimization)
C  short_circuit_disabled_in_max_allowed  11.3, 11.5
   In MAXIMUM_ALLOWED mode, walk runs to completion even if all desired bits decided
C  short_circuit_not_applied_with_tree  11.3, 11.17
   Short-circuit does not apply when object_tree is present
C  duplicate_guids_in_tree_rejected  11.3
   Object type list with duplicate GUIDs returns ERROR_INVALID_PARAMETER
C  level_gap_in_tree_rejected  11.3
   Object type list with level gap (level 3 after level 1) returns ERROR_INVALID_PARAMETER
### 11.4 Owner Implicit Rights
C  owner_gets_read_control_write_dac  11.4
   Owner receives READ_CONTROL and WRITE_DAC regardless of DACL contents
C  owner_implicit_before_dacl_walk  11.4
   Owner implicit rights are granted before the DACL walk (deny ACEs cannot override them)
C  owner_implicit_immune_to_deny_aces  11.4
   A deny ACE for READ_CONTROL/WRITE_DAC against the owner does not override implicit rights
C  owner_rights_sid_suppresses_implicit  11.4
   Presence of any ACE targeting S-1-3-4 (OWNER RIGHTS) in the DACL suppresses the implicit grant
C  owner_rights_deny_ace_suppresses_implicit  11.4
   A deny ACE targeting OWNER RIGHTS suppresses implicit grant (mere presence triggers suppression)
C  owner_rights_prescan_ignores_inherit_only  11.4
   Pre-scan for OWNER RIGHTS skips inherit-only ACEs
C  owner_rights_prescan_ignores_non_access_control  11.4
   Pre-scan for OWNER RIGHTS ignores non-access-control ACE types (e.g., audit ACEs in SACL)
C  owner_rights_prescan_checks_presence_not_condition  11.4, 11.12
   Pre-scan checks for ACE presence only, not conditional expression result
C  owner_rights_allow_ace_narrows_access  11.4
   OWNER RIGHTS allow ACE with only READ_CONTROL: owner gets READ_CONTROL but not WRITE_DAC
C  owner_rights_allow_ace_expands_access  11.4
   OWNER RIGHTS allow ACE with READ_CONTROL+WRITE_DAC+DELETE: owner gets more than default
C  owner_rights_sid_matches_owner_in_walk  11.4
   During DACL walk, S-1-3-4 ACEs match the owner as if they were normal SID ACEs
C  owner_rights_not_exclusive_channel  11.4
   Owner also receives access from ACEs matching their user/group SIDs in addition to S-1-3-4
C  owner_empty_dacl_gets_implicit_rights_only  11.3, 11.4
   Owner with empty DACL receives only READ_CONTROL+WRITE_DAC (from implicit rights)
C  owner_implicit_rights_on_tree_nodes  11.4, 11.17
   Owner implicit rights (READ_CONTROL+WRITE_DAC) are applied to all tree nodes
### 11.5 MAXIMUM_ALLOWED
C  max_allowed_stripped_before_evaluation  11.5
   MAXIMUM_ALLOWED bit is stripped from desired mask before evaluation
C  max_allowed_not_a_right  11.5
   MAXIMUM_ALLOWED cannot appear in an ACE mask
C  max_allowed_returns_full_effective_mask  11.5
   MAXIMUM_ALLOWED mode returns the complete set of rights the pipeline accumulated
C  max_allowed_no_short_circuit  11.5
   MAXIMUM_ALLOWED mode: DACL walk runs to completion (all ACEs evaluated)
C  max_allowed_combined_with_specific_rights  READ_CONTROL: allowed reflects whether READ_CONTROL granted; granted reflects full mask
   MAXIMUM_ALLOWED
C  max_allowed_with_ass_without_privilege  ACCESS_SYSTEM_SECURITY without SeSecurityPrivilege: allowed=false, granted has everything else
   MAXIMUM_ALLOWED
C  pure_max_allowed_always_succeeds  11.5
   Pure MAXIMUM_ALLOWED with no specific bits always returns allowed=true
C  pure_max_allowed_zero_granted_succeeds  11.5
   Pure MAXIMUM_ALLOWED that produces zero granted returns allowed=true (not an error)
C  max_allowed_first_writer_wins_same_as_targeted  11.5
   MAXIMUM_ALLOWED uses same first-writer-wins as targeted requests (no accumulate-and-subtract)
C  max_allowed_agrees_with_targeted_on_noncanonical_dacl  11.5
   On non-canonical DACL, MAXIMUM_ALLOWED and targeted request agree (Peios divergence from Windows)
C  zero_desired_mask_succeeds  11.5, 11.17
   Zero desired mask (no rights requested) returns allowed=true
### 11.6 Privileges in AccessCheck
#### SeSecurityPrivilege / ACCESS_SYSTEM_SECURITY
C  ass_granted_with_security_privilege  11.6
   ACCESS_SYSTEM_SECURITY granted when SeSecurityPrivilege is present and enabled
C  ass_denied_without_security_privilege  11.6
   ACCESS_SYSTEM_SECURITY denied when SeSecurityPrivilege is absent
C  ass_always_decided_before_dacl  11.6
   ACCESS_SYSTEM_SECURITY is always decided before the DACL walk
C  ass_no_dacl_ace_can_grant_it  11.6
   No DACL ACE can grant ACCESS_SYSTEM_SECURITY (bit always resolved before walk)
C  ass_no_dacl_ace_can_deny_it  11.6
   No DACL ACE can deny ACCESS_SYSTEM_SECURITY (already decided)
C  ass_denial_no_early_out  11.6
   Missing SeSecurityPrivilege does not cause an early-out; denial falls out from final result computation
C  ass_tracked_in_privilege_granted  11.6
   ACCESS_SYSTEM_SECURITY grant is tracked in privilege_granted mask
C  ass_tracked_in_security_provenance  11.17
   ACCESS_SYSTEM_SECURITY is attributed to SeSecurityPrivilege in provenance
#### SeTakeOwnershipPrivilege
C  take_ownership_grants_write_owner_if_dacl_did_not  11.6
   SeTakeOwnershipPrivilege grants WRITE_OWNER only if the DACL did not independently grant it
C  take_ownership_silent_when_dacl_granted  11.6
   If DACL granted WRITE_OWNER, SeTakeOwnershipPrivilege stays silent (not exercised, not audited)
C  take_ownership_post_dacl_position  11.6, 11.17
   SeTakeOwnershipPrivilege is evaluated after the DACL walk (step 7a)
C  take_ownership_overrides_dacl_deny  11.6, 11.17
   SeTakeOwnershipPrivilege overrides a DACL deny ACE for WRITE_OWNER (deny-proof)
C  take_ownership_respects_mic_mandatory_decided  11.6, 11.17
   SeTakeOwnershipPrivilege does NOT override MIC-decided WRITE_OWNER (checks mandatory_decided)
C  take_ownership_respects_pip_mandatory_decided  11.6, 11.17
   SeTakeOwnershipPrivilege does NOT override PIP-decided WRITE_OWNER
C  take_ownership_tracked_in_privilege_granted  11.6, 11.17
   WRITE_OWNER granted by SeTakeOwnershipPrivilege tracked in privilege_granted
C  take_ownership_in_max_allowed_mode  11.17
   In MAXIMUM_ALLOWED mode, SeTakeOwnershipPrivilege is evaluated (WRITE_OWNER or max_allowed_mode guard)
C  take_ownership_updates_tree_nodes  11.17
   SeTakeOwnershipPrivilege grants WRITE_OWNER to all tree nodes that lack it
#### SeBackupPrivilege / SeRestorePrivilege
C  backup_privilege_grants_all_read_bits  11.6
   SeBackupPrivilege grants MapGenericBits(GENERIC_READ, mapping)
C  restore_privilege_grants_all_write_bits_plus_extras  WRITE_DAC
   SeRestorePrivilege grants MapGenericBits(GENERIC_WRITE)
C  backup_intent_gated  11.6
   SeBackupPrivilege is invisible without BACKUP_INTENT flag
C  restore_intent_gated  11.6
   SeRestorePrivilege is invisible without RESTORE_INTENT flag
C  backup_with_intent_grants_rights  11.6
   SeBackupPrivilege + BACKUP_INTENT grants all read-mapped bits
C  restore_with_intent_grants_rights  11.6
   SeRestorePrivilege + RESTORE_INTENT grants all write-mapped bits plus extras
C  backup_without_intent_invisible  11.6
   Token has SeBackupPrivilege but no BACKUP_INTENT: backup bits not granted
C  restore_without_intent_invisible  11.6
   Token has SeRestorePrivilege but no RESTORE_INTENT: restore bits not granted
C  intent_gated_inside_pipeline_not_bypass  11.6
   Backup/restore privileges are evaluated inside AccessCheck, not as a short-circuit bypass
C  backup_bits_tracked_in_privilege_granted  11.17
   Bits from SeBackupPrivilege tracked in privilege_granted and backup_granted provenance
C  restore_bits_tracked_in_privilege_granted  11.17
   Bits from SeRestorePrivilege tracked in privilege_granted and restore_granted provenance
#### SeRelabelPrivilege
C  relabel_privilege_loosens_mic_for_write_owner  11.6, 11.13
   SeRelabelPrivilege allows WRITE_OWNER through MIC even when caller is non-dominant
C  relabel_privilege_does_not_grant_directly  11.6
   SeRelabelPrivilege does not grant any access rights directly (only loosens MIC)
C  relabel_audit_when_write_owner_granted_and_no_take_ownership  11.17
   SeRelabelPrivilege audit fires when WRITE_OWNER granted AND SeTakeOwnershipPrivilege did not claim it
### 11.7 Restricted Tokens
C  restricted_token_two_pass_evaluation  11.7
   Restricted token: DACL evaluated twice (normal pass and restricted pass)
C  restricted_intersection_normal_and_restricted  11.7
   Final granted = intersection of normal pass and restricted pass
C  restricted_pass_matches_only_restricting_sids  11.7
   Restricted pass: ACE matches only if its SID appears in restricting SID list
C  restricted_caps_access  11.7
   Normal pass grants READ+WRITE, restricted grants only READ: final is READ only
C  write_restricted_intersection_only_write_bits  11.7
   Write-restricted token: intersection applies only to write-category bits (from GENERIC_WRITE mapping)
C  write_restricted_read_from_normal_pass_only  11.7
   Write-restricted token: read/execute access comes from normal pass alone
C  privilege_granted_bypass_restricted  11.7
   Privilege-granted bits are OR'd back after intersection (privileges bypass restricted pass)
C  owner_implicit_rights_in_restricted_pass  11.7
   Restricted pass grants owner implicit rights if owner SID is in restricting SID list
C  restricted_pass_no_owner_implicit_if_owner_not_restricting  11.7
   Restricted pass does NOT grant owner implicit rights if owner SID is NOT in restricting SID list
C  restricted_pass_owner_rights_suppression  11.7
   Restricted pass independently evaluates OWNER RIGHTS suppression
C  restricted_pass_fresh_tree  11.17
   Restricted pass starts with fresh decided=0/granted=0 per tree node
C  restricted_tree_merge_per_node  11.17
   Tree merge: per-node intersection between normal and restricted pass
C  restricted_tree_privilege_orback  11.17
   Tree merge: privilege_granted OR'd back into each node after intersection
C  write_restricted_tree_merge  11.17
   Write-restricted tree merge: intersection only on write-category bits per node
C  restricted_virtual_groups_injected  11.17
   Restricted pass injects S-1-3-4 if owner in restricting SIDs, S-1-5-10 if self_sid in restricting SIDs
C  restricted_device_groups_swapped  11.17
   Restricted pass: if token has restricted_device_groups, conditional expressions see restricted set
C  deny_only_group_in_restricted_context  11.7
   Deny-only groups reduce normal pass grants via deny ACEs (different from restricting SIDs which add a second eval)
### 11.8 Object ACEs and Property-Level Access
C  object_ace_without_guid_is_basic_ace  11.8
   Object ACE without ACE_OBJECT_TYPE_PRESENT behaves as a basic ACE (whole object)
C  object_ace_with_guid_targets_specific_node  11.8
   Object ACE with GUID updates only the targeted tree node (and propagation targets)
C  object_ace_guid_ignored_without_tree  11.8
   Object ACE with GUID but no object_tree: GUID ignored, treated as basic ACE
C  object_ace_guid_not_in_tree_skipped  11.8, 11.17
   Object ACE whose GUID does not match any tree node is skipped (FindNode returns null)
C  downward_grant_propagation  11.8
   Allow object ACE on property set grants to all child attributes
C  downward_grant_respects_first_writer_wins  11.8
   Downward grant does not override a child attribute that was already denied by an earlier ACE
C  upward_grant_aggregation  11.8
   When all siblings share a granted right, it propagates up to the parent node
C  upward_grant_per_bit_intersection  11.8
   Upward propagation uses per-bit intersection: right propagates to parent only if ALL siblings share it
C  upward_grant_propagation_to_root  11.8
   Aggregation continues upward to root: if every property set has a right, root gets it
C  upward_grant_stops_if_not_all_siblings  11.8, 11.17
   Upward propagation stops if not all siblings share the granted right
C  upward_deny_propagation_unconditional  11.8
   Deny object ACE on a child: denial propagates upward unconditionally to parent and root
C  upward_deny_does_not_affect_siblings  11.8
   Upward deny propagation does not affect sibling nodes
C  downward_deny_propagation  11.8
   Deny object ACE on property set: denial flows to all child attributes
C  downward_deny_respects_first_writer_wins  11.8
   Downward deny does not override child attributes already granted by earlier ACE
C  non_object_ace_affects_all_nodes  11.8
   Basic (non-object) ACE affects all tree nodes
#### PRINCIPAL_SELF
C  principal_self_matches_caller_who_is_object_principal  11.8
   ACE targeting S-1-5-10 matches when caller's token represents the same principal as object
C  principal_self_no_match_without_self_sid  11.8
   If self_sid is null, PRINCIPAL_SELF ACEs match nothing
C  principal_self_deny_only_allow_deny_asymmetry  11.8
   If caller matches self_sid via deny-only SID, S-1-5-10 matches for deny ACEs but not allow ACEs
C  principal_self_in_basic_ace  11.8
   PRINCIPAL_SELF (S-1-5-10) can appear in basic ACEs (not just object ACEs)
C  principal_self_inject_via_enrich_token  11.17
   EnrichToken injects S-1-5-10 as virtual group when self_sid matches caller
C  principal_self_deny_only_virtual_group  11.17
   EnrichToken: if self_sid matches only via deny SID match, S-1-5-10 injected as deny_only virtual group
#### Object Type List Validation
C  tree_empty_rejected  11.17
   Empty object_tree returns ERROR_INVALID_PARAMETER
C  tree_root_not_level_zero_rejected  11.17
   Object tree where first node is not level 0 returns ERROR_INVALID_PARAMETER
C  tree_negative_level_rejected  11.17
   Object tree with negative level returns ERROR_INVALID_PARAMETER
C  tree_multiple_level_zero_rejected  11.17
   Object tree with more than one level-0 node returns ERROR_INVALID_PARAMETER
C  tree_level_gap_rejected  11.17
   Object tree with node at level N+2 following level N (gap) returns ERROR_INVALID_PARAMETER
C  tree_duplicate_guids_rejected  11.17
   Object tree with duplicate GUIDs returns ERROR_INVALID_PARAMETER
C  tree_initialization_copies_scalar_state  11.17
   Tree initialization copies scalar decided/granted to each node
### 11.10 Auditing
C  audit_ace_does_not_affect_access_decision  11.10
   Audit ACE never grants or denies rights (purely observational)
C  audit_ace_success_flag_gates_success_audit  11.10
   SUCCESSFUL_ACCESS_ACE_FLAG controls whether successful access is audited
C  audit_ace_failure_flag_gates_failure_audit  11.10
   FAILED_ACCESS_ACE_FLAG controls whether failed access is audited
C  audit_ace_both_flags_audits_everything  11.10
   ACE with both success and failure flags audits all matching access attempts
C  audit_sid_matches_with_deny_polarity  11.10
   Audit ACE SID matching uses deny polarity (broadest identity view)
C  audit_inherit_only_skipped  11.10
   Audit ACE with INHERIT_ONLY is skipped
C  audit_no_flags_skipped  11.10
   Audit ACE with neither success nor failure flag is skipped
C  audit_conditional_unknown_fires  11.10, 11.12
   Conditional audit ACE: UNKNOWN condition fires the event (when in doubt, audit)
C  audit_conditional_false_skipped  11.10, 11.12
   Conditional audit ACE: FALSE condition skips the event
C  audit_object_per_node_success  11.10, 11.17
   Object-scoped audit ACE: success computed per-node, not whole object
C  continuous_audit_alarm_ace_builds_mask  11.10
   SYSTEM_ALARM ACE builds continuous_audit_mask on successful access
C  continuous_audit_only_on_success  11.10
   Continuous audit (alarm ACEs) only evaluated on successful access
C  continuous_audit_intersect_with_granted  11.10
   Continuous audit mask intersected with granted rights (only audit what the handle can do)
C  privilege_use_audit_only_when_necessary  11.10, 11.17
   Privilege-use audit fires only when the privilege was actually necessary for the final result
C  privilege_use_audit_not_in_max_allowed  11.17
   Privilege-use auditing does not fire in MAXIMUM_ALLOWED mode
C  privilege_use_audit_after_cap_and_pip  11.10, 11.17
   Privilege-use audit fires after the complete pipeline (after CAP/PIP may have revoked bits)
C  per_token_audit_policy_success  11.17
   Token audit_policy.object_access_success fires unconditionally regardless of SACL
C  per_token_audit_policy_failure  11.17
   Token audit_policy.object_access_failure fires unconditionally regardless of SACL
### 11.11 Resource Attributes
C  resource_attrs_extracted_before_dacl_walk  11.11
   Resource attributes from SACL are available when conditional expressions need them
C  resource_attr_first_name_wins  11.11
   If two resource attribute ACEs have the same name, the first one wins
C  resource_attr_does_not_grant_deny  11.11
   Resource attributes do not directly grant or deny access
C  resource_attr_available_to_conditional_dacl  11.11, 11.12
   Resource attributes are available to conditional expressions in DACL ACEs
C  resource_attr_available_to_conditional_audit  11.11, 11.10
   Resource attributes are available to conditional audit ACEs in the SACL
### 11.12 Conditional ACEs
#### Condition Evaluation Three-Value Logic
C  conditional_allow_fires_only_on_true  11.12
   Conditional allow ACE takes effect only when condition evaluates to TRUE
C  conditional_allow_skipped_on_false  11.12
   Conditional allow ACE skipped when condition is FALSE
C  conditional_allow_skipped_on_unknown  11.12
   Conditional allow ACE skipped when condition is UNKNOWN
C  conditional_deny_fires_on_true  11.12
   Conditional deny ACE takes effect when condition is TRUE
C  conditional_deny_fires_on_unknown  11.12
   Conditional deny ACE takes effect when condition is UNKNOWN (fail-safe)
C  conditional_deny_skipped_on_false  11.12
   Conditional deny ACE skipped only when condition is FALSE
C  three_value_and_false_false  11.12
   AND: both FALSE = FALSE
C  three_value_and_true_true  11.12
   AND: both TRUE = TRUE
C  three_value_and_true_false  11.12
   AND: TRUE and FALSE = FALSE
C  three_value_and_true_unknown  11.12
   AND: TRUE and UNKNOWN = UNKNOWN
C  three_value_and_false_unknown  11.12
   AND: FALSE and UNKNOWN = FALSE
C  three_value_and_unknown_unknown  11.12
   AND: UNKNOWN and UNKNOWN = UNKNOWN
C  three_value_or_true_true  11.12
   OR: both TRUE = TRUE
C  three_value_or_false_false  11.12
   OR: both FALSE = FALSE
C  three_value_or_true_false  11.12
   OR: TRUE and FALSE = TRUE
C  three_value_or_true_unknown  11.12
   OR: TRUE and UNKNOWN = TRUE
C  three_value_or_false_unknown  11.12
   OR: FALSE and UNKNOWN = UNKNOWN
C  three_value_or_unknown_unknown  11.12
   OR: UNKNOWN and UNKNOWN = UNKNOWN
C  three_value_not_true  11.12
   NOT TRUE = FALSE
C  three_value_not_false  11.12
   NOT FALSE = TRUE
C  three_value_not_unknown  11.12
   NOT UNKNOWN = UNKNOWN
#### Boolean Coercion
C  bool_coerce_int_nonzero_true  11.12
   INT64/UINT64 nonzero coerces to TRUE for logical operators
C  bool_coerce_int_zero_false  11.12
   INT64/UINT64 zero coerces to FALSE
C  bool_coerce_string_nonempty_true  11.12
   Non-empty STRING coerces to TRUE
C  bool_coerce_string_empty_false  11.12
   Empty STRING coerces to FALSE
C  bool_coerce_null_unknown  11.12
   NULL coerces to UNKNOWN
C  bool_coerce_sid_unknown  11.12
   SID coerces to UNKNOWN (not boolean)
C  bool_coerce_octet_unknown  11.12
   OCTET coerces to UNKNOWN (not boolean)
C  bool_coerce_composite_unknown  11.12
   COMPOSITE coerces to UNKNOWN (not boolean)
C  literal_in_logical_context_unknown  11.12
   Literal-origin values in logical operators produce UNKNOWN (literals are not boolean propositions)
#### Attribute Resolution
C  user_attr_resolves_from_token  11.12
   @User. prefix resolves from token.user_claims
C  device_attr_resolves_from_token  11.12
   @Device. prefix resolves from token.device_claims
C  resource_attr_resolves_from_sacl  11.12, 11.11
   @Resource. prefix resolves from SACL resource attributes
C  local_attr_resolves_from_parameter  11.12
   @Local. prefix resolves from AccessCheck parameter (not token)
C  missing_device_claims_resolve_absent  11.12
   @Device. references resolve as absent (NULL) when device claims not populated
#### Claim Flags
C  disabled_claim_invisible  11.12
   DISABLED flag (0x0010) makes attribute invisible to all conditions (resolves as NULL)
C  deny_only_claim_invisible_to_allow  11.12
   USE_FOR_DENY_ONLY (0x0004) claim resolves as absent for allow ACE conditions
C  deny_only_claim_visible_to_deny  11.12
   USE_FOR_DENY_ONLY claim is visible to deny ACE conditions
C  deny_only_resource_attr_invisible_to_allow  11.12
   USE_FOR_DENY_ONLY on a resource attribute: invisible to allow-ACE conditions
C  empty_attr_normalized_to_null  11.12
   Attribute with zero values normalized to absent (NULL) at resolution time
C  exists_false_for_empty_attr  11.12
   Exists returns FALSE for empty attributes (normalized to NULL)
C  empty_attr_deny_unknown_fires  11.12
   Empty attribute on deny ACE condition: evaluates to UNKNOWN, deny fires (fail-safe)
#### Conditional OWNER RIGHTS
C  conditional_owner_rights_suppresses_even_if_false  11.12, 11.4
   Conditional ACE targeting S-1-3-4 suppresses implicit grant even if condition evaluates to FALSE
C  conditional_owner_rights_lockout_scenario  11.12
   Conditional OWNER RIGHTS with FALSE condition: owner loses implicit rights AND gets nothing from ACE
#### Virtual Groups in Expressions
C  member_of_owner_rights_true_for_owner  11.12
   Member_of({S-1-3-4}) returns TRUE when caller is the owner (virtual group visible)
C  member_of_principal_self_true_for_self  11.12
   Member_of({S-1-5-10}) returns TRUE when caller matches self_sid
C  virtual_groups_visible_to_expressions  11.12
   Conditional expressions see virtual groups injected by EnrichToken
#### Expression Evaluation Edge Cases
C  sid_match_before_condition_eval  11.12
   SID is matched first; condition expression evaluated only if SID matches
C  conditional_object_ace_combines_condition_and_guid  11.12, 11.8
   ACCESS_ALLOWED_CALLBACK_OBJECT combines conditional expression with property-level GUID targeting
C  callback_ace_no_condition_data_returns_unknown  11.12, 11.17
   Callback allow ACE with null condition data evaluates as UNKNOWN (skipped)
C  callback_ace_means_conditional  11.12
   Callback ACE types exist solely to carry conditional expressions in Peios (no Windows callback mechanism)
C  int64_uint64_promotion  11.12
   INT64 vs UINT64 comparison: negative INT64 always less than any UINT64, overlapping range compared as integers (Peios divergence)
C  member_of_polarity_aware  11.12
   Member_of filters deny-only groups by ACE polarity (Peios divergence from MS-DTYP)
C  exists_extended_to_all_namespaces  11.12
   Exists/Not_Exists extended to all four namespaces (@User., @Device., @Local., @Resource.)
C  composite_equality_element_wise  11.12
   Composite-vs-composite equality uses element-wise ordering (same length, order, elements)
C  expression_magic_header_required  11.17
   Expression must start with artx magic bytes [0x61, 0x72, 0x74, 0x78]; else UNKNOWN
C  expression_stack_not_one_at_end_unknown  11.17
   If stack does not have exactly one element after full evaluation, return UNKNOWN
C  expression_final_literal_returns_unknown  11.17
   If final stack element has origin=LITERAL, return UNKNOWN
C  expression_bounds_violation_unknown  11.17
   Any read beyond condition buffer bounds returns UNKNOWN
C  expression_unknown_opcode_unknown  11.17
   Unknown opcode returns UNKNOWN
C  expression_insufficient_stack_unknown  11.17
   Operator with insufficient stack operands returns UNKNOWN
C  exists_requires_attr_origin  11.17
   Exists/Not_Exists: operand must have attribute origin (LOCAL_ATTR, RESOURCE_ATTR, USER_ATTR, DEVICE_ATTR); else UNKNOWN
C  member_of_all_sids_required  11.17
   Member_of requires ALL SIDs in the list to match the token (conjunction)
C  member_of_any_any_sid_sufficient  11.17
   Member_of_Any requires ANY SID in the list to match (disjunction)
C  device_member_of_null_device_groups_unknown  11.17
   Device_Member_of with null device_groups: returns UNKNOWN
C  not_member_of_negates_member_of  11.17
   Not_Member_of is logical negation of Member_of
C  to_sid_list_empty_composite_error  11.17
   to_sid_list with empty composite returns error (UNKNOWN in context)
C  to_sid_list_non_sid_element_error  11.17
   to_sid_list with non-SID element in composite returns error
C  compare_equal_null_unknown  11.17
   compare_equal: NULL operand returns UNKNOWN
C  compare_equal_scalar_vs_composite_unknown  11.17
   compare_equal: scalar vs composite returns UNKNOWN
C  compare_equal_type_mismatch_unknown  11.17
   compare_equal: incompatible types return UNKNOWN
C  string_compare_case_insensitive_default  11.17
   String comparison is case-insensitive by default (ASCII folding only)
C  string_compare_case_sensitive_flag  11.17
   CASE_SENSITIVE flag (0x0002) on either operand forces case-sensitive comparison
C  boolean_normalized_on_resolution  11.17
   BOOLEAN values normalized to 1/0 at resolution time regardless of wire encoding
C  resolve_claim_case_insensitive_lookup  11.17
   Claim resolution uses case-insensitive name lookup
C  resolve_claim_null_claims_returns_null  11.17
   resolve_claim with null claims source returns Value(NULL)
C  resolve_claim_name_not_found_returns_null  11.17
   resolve_claim for missing name returns Value(NULL)
C  multi_valued_claim_returns_composite  11.17
   Claim with multiple values resolves as COMPOSITE
C  single_valued_claim_returns_scalar  11.17
   Claim with single value resolves as scalar of the appropriate type
C  integer_literal_sign_byte_determines_signedness  11.17
   Int literal: sign byte (0x02) alone determines negative; magnitude is unsigned
### 11.13 Mandatory Integrity Control (MIC)
C  mic_no_write_up_default  11.13
   Default MIC: no-write-up blocks write-mapped bits for non-dominant callers
C  mic_dominant_caller_bypasses  11.13
   Caller at or above object's integrity level: MIC imposes no restrictions
C  mic_non_dominant_blocks_writes  11.13
   Non-dominant caller (integrity below object): write bits blocked regardless of DACL
C  mic_no_read_up_flag  11.13
   SYSTEM_MANDATORY_LABEL_NO_READ_UP: read bits blocked for non-dominant callers
C  mic_no_execute_up_flag  11.13
   SYSTEM_MANDATORY_LABEL_NO_EXECUTE_UP: execute bits blocked for non-dominant callers
C  mic_all_three_flags  11.13
   All three MIC flags set: non-dominant caller gets no read, write, or execute access
C  mic_default_label_medium  11.13
   Object without mandatory label ACE: default is Medium integrity with NO_WRITE_UP
C  mic_default_protects_from_low  11.13
   Default Medium label: Low-integrity process cannot write to unlabeled objects
C  mic_default_protects_from_untrusted  11.13
   Default Medium label: Untrusted process cannot write to unlabeled objects
C  mic_does_not_constrain_privileges  11.13
   MIC does not revoke privilege-granted bits (privileges resolved before MIC)
C  mic_token_mandatory_policy_flag  11.13
   MIC enforced only when TOKEN_MANDATORY_POLICY_NO_WRITE_UP flag is set
C  mic_policy_cleared_disables_mic  11.13
   TOKEN_MANDATORY_POLICY_NO_WRITE_UP cleared: MIC not enforced (token can write up)
C  mic_policy_bitmask_check  11.13
   Mandatory policy checked as bitmask (& NO_WRITE_UP), not equality
P  mic_policy_immutable  11.13
   Mandatory policy is set at token creation, cannot be modified at runtime (Peios divergence)
C  mic_only_first_label_matters  11.13
   Multiple mandatory label ACEs: only the first one is used
C  mic_inherit_only_label_skipped  11.13, 11.17
   Mandatory label ACE with INHERIT_ONLY is skipped (not used for MIC evaluation)
C  mic_non_dominant_allowed_starts_read_execute  11.17
   Non-dominant MIC: allowed starts with R+E, then stripped by flags
C  mic_serelabel_allows_write_owner_through  11.13
   SeRelabelPrivilege allows WRITE_OWNER in MIC allowed set even for non-dominant callers
C  mic_decided_bits_tracked_in_mandatory_decided  11.17
   MIC-decided bits are tracked in mandatory_decided for SeTakeOwnershipPrivilege gating
C  mic_integrity_levels_total_order  11.13
   System > High > Medium > Low > Untrusted is a strict total order
C  mic_equal_level_dominates  11.13
   Caller at same integrity level as object dominates (>= comparison)
### 11.14 Application Confinement
C  confinement_starts_from_nothing  11.14
   Confined token: default is deny; only confinement SID / capability SID ACEs grant access
C  confinement_intersection_with_normal  11.14
   Confinement result is intersection with normal evaluation (AND)
C  confinement_no_privilege_bypass  11.14
   Privileges do NOT bypass confinement (absolute boundary)
C  confinement_no_owner_implicit_rights  11.14
   Owner implicit rights skipped in confinement evaluation (skip_owner_implicit=true)
C  confinement_backup_privilege_blocked  11.14
   SeBackupPrivilege does NOT grant access through confinement boundary
C  confinement_take_ownership_blocked  11.14
   SeTakeOwnershipPrivilege does NOT grant WRITE_OWNER through confinement
C  confinement_security_privilege_blocked  11.14
   SeSecurityPrivilege / ACCESS_SYSTEM_SECURITY unreachable for confined tokens
C  confinement_exempt_skips_check  11.14
   confinement_exempt=true: confinement restrictions not evaluated
C  confinement_null_sid_means_not_confined  11.14
   confinement_sid=null: token is not confined, confinement not evaluated
C  confinement_matches_package_sid  11.14
   Confinement pass matches the token's confinement_sid against ACEs
C  confinement_matches_capability_sids  11.14
   Confinement pass matches confinement_capabilities against ACEs
C  confinement_matches_all_app_packages  11.14
   ALL_APPLICATION_PACKAGES SID in capabilities: normal confined token matches broad ACEs
C  strict_confinement_no_all_app_packages  11.14
   Strict confinement: token without ALL_APPLICATION_PACKAGES has much narrower access surface
C  confinement_null_dacl_grants_access  11.14
   Confined token with NULL DACL on object: confinement pass grants all valid bits (object opted in)
C  confinement_principal_self_isolated  11.14
   Confinement pass: S-1-5-10 injected only if self_sid matches a confinement SID, not user identity
C  confinement_conditional_sees_full_token  11.14
   Confinement pass: conditional expressions inside matched ACEs see user's real groups/claims
C  confinement_after_restricted_merge  11.14, 11.17
   Confinement runs AFTER restricted token merge and privilege OR-back (step 8a after step 8)
C  confinement_ordering_prevents_privilege_resurrection  11.17
   Ordering: privilege OR-back in step 8 cannot resurrect bits blocked by confinement in step 8a
C  confinement_tree_fresh_copy  11.17
   Confinement pass uses fresh tree copy (decided=0, granted=0 per node)
C  confinement_tree_intersection  11.17
   Confinement tree merge: per-node intersection with normal tree
C  confinement_virtual_groups_owner_in_sids  11.17
   Confinement pass injects S-1-3-4 if owner SID is in confinement SID list
C  confinement_virtual_groups_self_in_sids  11.17
   Confinement pass injects S-1-5-10 if self_sid is in confinement SID list
### 11.15 Process Integrity Protection (PIP)
C  pip_dominant_caller_unrestricted  11.15
   Caller dominates trust label: PIP imposes no restrictions
C  pip_non_dominant_restricted_to_ace_mask  11.15
   Non-dominant caller: only rights in trust label ACE mask are permitted
C  pip_dominance_requires_both_dimensions  11.15
   Dominance requires pip_type >= ace_type AND pip_trust >= ace_trust
C  pip_partial_order_incomparable  11.15
   Isolated trust-2 vs Protected trust-5: neither dominates (incomparable)
C  pip_higher_type_lower_trust_not_dominant  11.15
   Higher pip_type but lower pip_trust: does not dominate
C  pip_higher_trust_lower_type_not_dominant  11.15
   Higher pip_trust but lower pip_type: does not dominate
C  pip_equal_type_and_trust_dominates  11.15
   Equal pip_type and pip_trust: dominates (>= on both)
C  pip_revokes_privilege_granted_bits  11.15
   PIP revokes privilege-granted bits outside the allowed set (clears from granted AND privilege_granted)
C  pip_revokes_backup_privilege  11.15
   PIP strips SeBackupPrivilege-granted read access for non-dominant callers
C  pip_revokes_security_privilege  11.15
   PIP strips SeSecurityPrivilege-granted ACCESS_SYSTEM_SECURITY for non-dominant callers
C  pip_revokes_take_ownership_privilege  11.15
   PIP strips SeTakeOwnershipPrivilege-granted WRITE_OWNER for non-dominant callers
C  pip_no_default_label  11.15
   Objects without trust label ACE: PIP imposes no restrictions (any process can access)
C  pip_no_relabel_equivalent  11.15
   No privilege can compensate for insufficient PIP trust (no carve-out)
C  pip_only_first_trust_label  11.15
   Multiple trust label ACEs: only the first is used
C  pip_inherit_only_trust_label_skipped  11.15, 11.17
   Trust label ACE with INHERIT_ONLY is skipped
C  pip_mask_zero_total_lockout  11.15
   Trust label ACE mask of 0: non-dominant callers get no access at all
C  pip_ace_mask_generic_mapped  11.17
   Trust label ACE mask is mapped through MapGenericBits for concrete allowed set
C  pip_all_bits_include_ass  11.17
   PIP all_bits includes ACCESS_SYSTEM_SECURITY (to prevent SACL access for non-dominant callers)
C  pip_decided_tracked_in_mandatory_decided  11.17
   PIP-decided bits tracked in mandatory_decided
P  pip_from_psb_not_token  11.15
   PIP evaluation uses pip_type/pip_trust from PSB, not from the token (impersonation-independent)
C  pip_type_total_order  11.15
   pip_type: Isolated(1024) > Protected(512) > None(0)
C  pip_trust_total_order  11.15
   pip_trust values form total order: PeiosTcb(8192) > Peios(4096) > App(2048) > AntiMalware(1536) > Authenticode(1024) > None(0)
### 11.16 Central Access Policy (CAP)
C  cap_intersects_with_normal_result  11.16
   CAP result is AND (intersection) with normal DACL evaluation
C  cap_can_only_restrict_never_expand  11.16
   CAP can only further restrict access, never expand beyond DACL result
C  cap_multiple_policies_compose_safely  11.16
   Multiple scoped policy ACEs: each further restricts (AND of all)
C  cap_missing_policy_uses_recovery  11.16
   Unknown policy SID (not in kernel cache): recovery policy used
C  cap_recovery_grants_owner_admin_system  11.16

C  cap_recovery_no_worse_than_no_cap  11.16
   Recovery policy with DACL intersection: effective access no worse than having no CAP
C  cap_error_in_rule_fail_closed  11.16
   CAP rule evaluation error: denies all access except privilege-granted rights
C  cap_error_preserves_privilege_escape  11.16
   CAP rule error: SeSecurityPrivilege-granted bits preserved (admin can fix broken policy)
C  cap_applies_to_condition  11.16
   CAP rule applies_to condition gates which rules fire (TRUE = applies, else skip)
C  cap_applies_to_deny_polarity  11.16, 11.17
   CAP applies_to condition uses deny polarity (deny-only groups/claims visible)
C  cap_rule_full_pipeline  11.16, 11.17

C  cap_no_backup_restore_intent  11.16, 11.17
   CAP rule evaluation passes privilege_intent=0 (no backup/restore)
C  cap_staging_effective_and_staged  11.16
   CAP rules can have both effective_dacl and staged_dacl
C  cap_staging_difference_logged  11.16
   If effective and staged results differ, the difference is logged
C  cap_staging_no_access_impact  11.16
   Staged DACL is shadow-evaluated only; does not affect actual access decision
C  cap_rules_without_staged_contribute_to_both  11.16
   Rules without staged DACL: effective result used for both effective and staged running totals
C  cap_staged_error_fallback_to_effective  11.17
   If staged evaluation fails, fallback to effective result for staged total
C  cap_enriched_token_for_applies_to  11.17
   CAP applies_to expressions see enriched token (virtual groups S-1-3-4, S-1-5-10)
C  cap_scoped_policy_ace_inherit_only_skipped  11.17
   SYSTEM_SCOPED_POLICY_ID_ACE with INHERIT_ONLY is skipped
C  cap_non_intent_privileges_survive_and  11.17
   SeSecurityPrivilege/SeTakeOwnershipPrivilege survive CAP AND (present in both normal and CAP eval)
C  cap_intent_privileges_stripped  11.17
   Backup/restore privileges stripped in CAP rule evaluation (privilege_intent=0)
C  cap_staging_diff_property_level  11.17
   CAP staging differences detected at per-property (tree node) level

## Summary
**Total tests: 384**

- **Cargo tests (pure Rust logic, no kernel): 364**
- **Provium tests (require booted KACS kernel): 20**

Coverage by pipeline stage:
- API variants (11.1): 7
- Generic mapping (11.2): 11
- DACL walk core (11.3): 20
- Owner implicit rights (11.4): 14
- MAXIMUM_ALLOWED (11.5): 11
- Privileges (11.6): 31
- Restricted tokens (11.7): 17
- Object ACEs / trees (11.8): 22
- Auditing (11.10): 18
- Resource attributes (11.11): 5
- Conditional ACEs (11.12): 80
- MIC (11.13): 21
- Confinement (11.14): 22
- PIP (11.15): 22
- CAP (11.16): 22
- Pipeline integration / helpers (11.17): 41
- Provium-only: 20

The overwhelming majority are Cargo tests because the AccessCheck pipeline is pure evaluation logic operating on data structures (tokens, SDs, masks) -- exactly what can be tested in userspace with a kacs-core crate. Provium tests cover the kernel integration surface: syscall entry points, LSM hooks, FACS/registryd callers passing intent flags, runtime immutability invariants, and the CAP policy cache lifecycle.

# Section 11: AccessCheck (Second Half)
## 1. Restricted Token Two-Pass (ss11.7, lines 6247-6310)
### Scalar Merge
C  restricted_normal_intersection  ss11.7 6292
   When a token has restricted SIDs and is NOT write-restricted, granted = normal_granted AND restricted_granted (bitwise intersection)
C  restricted_write_only_intersection  ss11.7 6287-6290
   When a token is write-restricted, only write-mapped bits are intersected; non-write bits pass from the normal pass unmodified
C  restricted_write_bits_from_generic_mapping  ss11.7 6288
   Write bits for write-restricted merge are computed via MapGenericBits(GENERIC_WRITE, mapping)
C  restricted_write_restricted_formula  ss11.7 6289-6290
   Write-restricted merge: granted = (normal_granted AND NOT write_bits) OR (normal_granted AND restricted_granted AND write_bits)
C  restricted_privilege_granted_or_back  ss11.7 6293-6294
   After intersection, privilege_granted bits are OR'd back into granted (privileges bypass the restricted pass)
C  restricted_privilege_or_back_after_intersection  ss11.7 6293-6294
   Privilege OR-back happens after the intersection, not before -- bits denied by restricted pass are restored by privilege
C  restricted_no_privilege_or_back_without_privileges  ss11.7 6294
   When privilege_granted is 0, OR-back adds nothing after intersection
### Virtual Groups in Restricted Pass
C  restricted_owner_virtual_group  ss11.7 6263-6264
   If sd.owner is in restricting_sids, SID_OWNER_RIGHTS is added to the restricted SID set
C  restricted_owner_not_in_restricting_sids  ss11.7 6263-6264
   If sd.owner is NOT in restricting_sids, SID_OWNER_RIGHTS is NOT added to the restricted set
C  restricted_principal_self_injection  ss11.7 6265-6267
   If self_sid is in restricting_sids, SID_PRINCIPAL_SELF is added to the restricted SID set
C  restricted_principal_self_not_in_restricting_sids  ss11.7 6265-6267
   If self_sid is NOT in restricting_sids, SID_PRINCIPAL_SELF is NOT added
C  restricted_principal_self_null_self_sid  ss11.7 6265-6267
   If self_sid is null, PRINCIPAL_SELF is never added to restricted set
### Restricted Device Groups
C  restricted_device_groups_swapped  ss11.7 6257-6259
   If token has restricted_device_groups, the restricted pass uses them instead of normal device_groups for conditional expression evaluation
C  restricted_device_groups_null_no_swap  ss11.7 6257-6259
   If restricted_device_groups is null, restricted pass uses normal device_groups
### Restricted Pass SID Matching
C  restricted_sid_match_uses_sid_list  ss11.7 6278-6279
   Restricted pass SID matching uses SidInRestrictingSids (list membership), not SidMatchesToken (group/deny-only filtering)
C  restricted_sid_match_ignores_for_allow  ss11.7 6278
   Restricted pass SID matching ignores the for_allow parameter (both allow and deny ACEs matched the same way)
### Tree Merge
C  restricted_tree_fresh_copy  ss11.7 6270-6276
   Restricted pass uses a deep copy of the object tree with decided=0, granted=0 on each node
C  restricted_tree_normal_intersection  ss11.7 6305-6307
   Non-write-restricted: each node.granted = normal_node.granted AND restricted_node.granted
C  restricted_tree_write_only_intersection  ss11.7 6298-6303
   Write-restricted: each node uses the write-bit formula for intersection
C  restricted_tree_privilege_or_back  ss11.7 6308-6309
   After tree merge, privilege_granted is OR'd back into every node's granted
C  restricted_tree_null_no_tree_merge  ss11.7 6270-6276, 6297
   When object_tree is null, tree merge is skipped
### Owner Implicit Rights in Restricted Pass
C  restricted_owner_implicit_rights  ss11.7 6283
   Restricted pass evaluates owner implicit rights independently (skip_owner_implicit=false)
C  restricted_owner_in_restricting_sids_gets_implicit  ss11.7 narrative 4740-4747
   If owner SID is a restricting SID, restricted pass grants READ_CONTROL and WRITE_DAC implicitly
C  restricted_owner_not_in_restricting_sids_no_implicit  ss11.7 narrative 4745-4747
   If owner SID is NOT a restricting SID, restricted pass does not grant implicit rights, reducing effective owner access via intersection

## 2. Confinement (ss11.14, lines 6311-6352)
### Core Behavior
C  confinement_absolute_intersection  ss11.14 6346-6347
   Confinement intersects with NO privilege bypass: granted = granted AND c_granted
C  confinement_no_privilege_bypass  ss11.14 6346-6347, narrative 5473
   Privilege-granted bits are NOT OR'd back after confinement intersection (unlike restricted tokens)
C  confinement_runs_after_restricted_merge  ss11.14 6311-6316
   Confinement runs AFTER restricted merge and its privilege OR-back (ordering critical)
C  confinement_ordering_prevents_privilege_resurrection  ss11.14 6314-6316
   If confinement ran before restricted, the privilege OR-back in step 8 would resurrect bits that confinement blocked
C  confinement_skip_owner_implicit  ss11.14 6343
   Confinement evaluation calls EvaluateDACL with skip_owner_implicit=true (owner does not get implicit rights in confinement pass)
C  confinement_not_active_when_null  ss11.14 6317
   When confinement_sid is null, confinement is not evaluated
C  confinement_exempt_skips_evaluation  ss11.14 6317
   When confinement_exempt is true, confinement is not evaluated even if confinement_sid is set
### Confinement SID Set
C  confinement_sid_set_package_plus_capabilities  ss11.14 6321-6322
   Confinement SID set = [confinement_sid] + confinement_capabilities
C  confinement_owner_rights_injection  ss11.14 6323-6324
   If sd.owner is in confinement_sids list, SID_OWNER_RIGHTS is added to confinement set
C  confinement_principal_self_injection  ss11.14 6325-6327
   If self_sid is in confinement_sids list, SID_PRINCIPAL_SELF is added to confinement set
C  confinement_principal_self_null_no_injection  ss11.14 6325-6327
   If self_sid is null, PRINCIPAL_SELF is not added to confinement set
C  confinement_sid_match_uses_sid_in_list  ss11.14 6329-6330
   Confinement SID matching uses SidInList (simple list membership), not SidMatchesToken
### Confinement Tree Handling
C  confinement_tree_deep_copy  ss11.14 6332-6338
   Confinement pass uses a deep copy of the object tree with decided=0, granted=0
C  confinement_tree_intersection  ss11.14 6349-6351
   Each node: object_tree[i].granted = normal_tree[i].granted AND c_tree[i].granted
C  confinement_tree_null_no_tree  ss11.14 6332-6338, 6348
   When object_tree is null, tree intersection is skipped
### Known Consequences (narrative)
C  confinement_sacl_access_unreachable  ss11.14 narrative 5519-5521
   ACCESS_SYSTEM_SECURITY is unreachable for confined tokens (privilege-only, privileges don't bypass confinement)
C  confinement_null_dacl_grants_access  ss11.14 narrative 5529-5535
   Object with NULL DACL grants access even in confinement pass (follows standard evaluation)
C  confinement_principal_self_isolated_from_user  ss11.14 narrative 5537-5543
   PRINCIPAL_SELF is only injected if self_sid matches a confinement SID; user SID match alone does not trigger it
C  confinement_conditional_sees_full_token  ss11.14 narrative 5545-5553
   Conditional expressions in confinement pass evaluate against the user's full token (groups, claims, device_claims)
C  confinement_all_app_packages_sid_match  ss11.14 narrative 5431-5432
   ACE with ALL_APPLICATION_PACKAGES SID matches when that SID is in confinement_capabilities
C  confinement_strict_no_all_app_packages  ss11.14 narrative 5491-5497
   Strictly confined token (no ALL_APPLICATION_PACKAGES in capabilities) does not match ALL_APPLICATION_PACKAGES ACEs

## 3. SeTakeOwnershipPrivilege Post-DACL (ss11.6/11.17, lines 6224-6246)
C  take_ownership_grants_write_owner_when_dacl_denies  ss11.6 6233-6240
   SeTakeOwnershipPrivilege grants WRITE_OWNER even when DACL denied it (deny-proof)
C  take_ownership_noop_when_dacl_grants  ss11.6 6235-6236

C  take_ownership_respects_mandatory_mic  ss11.6 6235-6236
   SeTakeOwnershipPrivilege does NOT override MIC-decided WRITE_OWNER (checks mandatory_decided)
C  take_ownership_respects_mandatory_pip  ss11.6 6235-6236
   SeTakeOwnershipPrivilege does NOT override PIP-decided WRITE_OWNER (checks mandatory_decided)
C  take_ownership_sets_privilege_granted  ss11.6 6238-6240
   When fired, SeTakeOwnershipPrivilege sets privilege_granted and take_ownership_granted
C  take_ownership_updates_tree_nodes  ss11.6 6241-6245
   When object_tree is present, SeTakeOwnershipPrivilege grants WRITE_OWNER on each node that doesn't already have it
C  take_ownership_only_on_desired_or_max_allowed  ss11.6 6233
   SeTakeOwnershipPrivilege only fires when desired includes WRITE_OWNER or in MAXIMUM_ALLOWED mode
C  take_ownership_without_privilege_noop  ss11.6 6234
   Without SeTakeOwnershipPrivilege enabled, step 7a does nothing

## 4. Central Access Policy (ss11.16, lines 6396-6524)
### CAP AND Semantics
C  cap_intersects_with_normal_result  ss11.16 6455, 6520
   CAP result is AND'd with normal DACL result (cap can only further restrict)
C  cap_multiple_policies_compound_and  ss11.16 6410-6496
   Multiple scoped policy SIDs compound via AND (each further restricts)
C  cap_never_expands_access  ss11.16 narrative 5856-5860
   Even if CAP rule DACL is broader than object DACL, granted cannot exceed object DACL result
### Recovery Policy
C  cap_unknown_policy_uses_recovery  ss11.16 6413
   When policy SID lookup returns null, RECOVERY_POLICY is used
C  cap_recovery_policy_grants_admin  ss11.16 7728-7731

C  cap_recovery_policy_grants_system  ss11.16 7728-7731
   RECOVERY_POLICY grants GENERIC_ALL to LOCAL_SYSTEM (S-1-5-18)

   RECOVERY_POLICY grants GENERIC_ALL to OWNER_RIGHTS (S-1-3-4)
C  cap_recovery_generic_all_mapped  ss11.16 7732-7734
   RECOVERY_POLICY uses GENERIC_ALL in ACE masks, mapped via MapGenericBits for each object type
### Applies-To Evaluation
C  cap_applies_to_null_matches_all  ss11.16 6420-6421
   Rule with null applies_to condition matches all objects
C  cap_applies_to_true_matches  ss11.16 6421-6425
   Rule with applies_to that evaluates to TRUE is applied
C  cap_applies_to_false_skips  ss11.16 6425-6426

P  provium_mic_dominant_bypasses  ss11.13
   High-integrity process writes to Medium-integrity file normally
P  provium_pip_non_dominant_blocked  ss11.15
   Non-PIP process cannot access PIP-protected object
P  provium_pip_dominant_allowed  ss11.15
   PIP-dominant process accesses PIP-protected object normally
P  provium_pip_revokes_privileges  ss11.15
   PIP strips SeBackupPrivilege-granted read from non-dominant process
P  provium_zero_desired_succeeds  ss11.1
   kacs_access_check with desired=0 returns success
P  provium_maximum_allowed_returns_full_grant  ss11.5
   kacs_access_check with MAXIMUM_ALLOWED returns accumulated grant mask
P  provium_maximum_allowed_zero_grant_succeeds  ss11.5
   kacs_access_check with MAXIMUM_ALLOWED and nothing grantable returns success with granted=0
P  provium_identification_token_denied  ss12.1
   Impersonation at Identification level: access check returns ACCESS_DENIED
P  provium_anonymous_token_proceeds  ss12.1
   Anonymous impersonation token proceeds through pipeline (S-1-5-7)
P  provium_null_dacl_grants_all  ss11.3
   File with NULL DACL: all rights granted regardless of caller identity
P  provium_empty_dacl_only_owner_implicit  ss11.3/11.4
   File with empty DACL: only owner gets READ_CONTROL/WRITE_DAC
P  provium_owner_rights_ace_suppresses_implicit  ss11.4
   OWNER RIGHTS ACE in DACL suppresses owner's implicit rights
P  provium_access_audit_event_emitted  ss11.10
   SYSTEM_AUDIT ACE causes audit event emission on matching access
P  provium_continuous_audit_mask_on_handle  ss11.10
   SYSTEM_ALARM ACE produces continuous audit mask on opened handle
P  provium_privilege_use_audit_emitted  ss11.10
   Privilege-granted access emits privilege-use audit event
P  provium_resource_attribute_extraction  ss11.11
   Resource attributes parsed from SACL and available to conditional ACEs
P  provium_result_list_per_property  ss11.1
   AccessCheckResultList returns per-node verdicts for object tree
---

**Summary:** 460 total tests extracted.
- **426 Cargo tests** (pure evaluation logic, data structures, conditional expression parsing, comparison operators, three-value logic, tree helpers, SID matching, claim resolution, all merge/intersection algorithms)
- **34 Provium tests** (syscalls, LSM hooks, file operations, process management, credential lifecycle, audit event emission, handle-level behavior)
